        <h3> 
         <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-book" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
          <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M3 5h4v1H3V5zm0 3h4V7H3v1zm0 2h4V9H3v1zm11-5h-4v1h4V5zm0 2h-4v1h4V7zm0 2h-4v1h4V9zm2-6v9c0 .55-.45 1-1 1H9.5l-1 1-1-1H2c-.55 0-1-.45-1-1V3c0-.55.45-1 1-1h5.5l1 1 1-1H15c.55 0 1 .45 1 1zm-8 .5L7.5 3H2v9h6V3.5zm7-.5H9.5l-.5.5V12h6V3z" />
         </svg> README.md </h3> 
        <article class="markdown-body entry-content" itemprop="text"> 
         <p><a href="https://travis-ci.org/okta/okta-auth-js"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3cb966c3345cb647f5112fec7f276756d509e4dd/68747470733a2f2f7472617669732d63692e6f72672f6f6b74612f6f6b74612d617574682d6a732e7376673f6272616e63683d6d6173746572" alt="Build Status" data-canonical-src="https://travis-ci.org/okta/okta-auth-js.svg?branch=master" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p> 
         <h1><a id="user-content-introduction" class="anchor" href="#introduction" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Introduction</h1> 
         <p>The Okta Auth SDK builds on top of our <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html">Authentication API</a> and <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/oidc.html">OAuth 2.0 API</a> to enable you to create a fully branded sign-in experience using JavaScript.</p> 
         <p>For an overview of the client's features and authentication flows, check out <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/guides/okta_auth_sdk.html">our developer docs</a>.</p> 
         <p>Read our <a href="/okta/okta-auth-js/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md">contributing guidelines</a> if you wish to contribute.</p> 
         <h1><a id="user-content-table-of-contents" class="anchor" href="#table-of-contents" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>

         <h1><a id="user-content-install" class="anchor" href="#install" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Install</h1> 
         <p>You can include Okta Auth JS in your project either directly from the Okta CDN, or by packaging it with your app via our npm package, <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/@okta/okta-auth-js">@okta/okta-auth-js</a>.</p> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-using-the-okta-cdn" class="anchor" href="#using-the-okta-cdn" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Using the Okta CDN</h2> 
         <p>Loading our assets directly from the CDN is a good choice if you want an easy way to get started with okta-auth-js, and don't already have an existing build process that leverages <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/">npm</a> for external dependencies.</p> 
         <p>To use the CDN, include links to the JS and CSS files in your HTML:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic">
          <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">&lt;!--</span> Latest CDN production Javascript: 1.6.0 <span class="pl-c">--&gt;</span></span>
&lt;<span class="pl-ent">script</span>
  <span class="pl-e">src</span>=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://ok1static.oktacdn.com/assets/js/sdk/okta-auth-js/1.6.0/okta-auth-js.min.js<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>text/javascript<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>&gt;<span class="pl-s1">&lt;</span>/<span class="pl-ent">script</span>&gt;</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>The <code>okta-auth-js.min.js</code> file will expose a global <code>OktaAuth</code> object. Use it to bootstrap the client:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> authClient <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">OktaAuth</span>({<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> configOptions <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-using-the-npm-module" class="anchor" href="#using-the-npm-module" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Using the npm module</h2> 
         <p>Using our npm module is a good choice if:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li> <p>You have a build system in place where you manage dependencies with npm.</p> </li> 
          <li> <p>You do not want to load scripts directly from third party sites.</p> </li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>To install <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/@okta/okta-auth-js">@okta/okta-auth-js</a>:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell">
          <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run this command in your project root folder.</span>
[project-root-folder]$ npm install @okta/okta-auth-js --save</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>After running <code>npm install</code>:</p> 
         <p>The minified auth client will be installed to <code>node_modules/@okta/okta-auth-js/dist</code>. You can copy the <code>dist</code> contents to a publicly hosted directory. However, if you're using a bundler like <a href="https://webpack.github.io/">Webpack</a> or <a href="http://browserify.org/">Browserify</a>, you can simply import the module using CommonJS.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> OktaAuth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>@okta/okta-auth-js<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-k">var</span> authClient <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">OktaAuth</span>(<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> configOptions <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h1><a id="user-content-api" class="anchor" href="#api" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>API</h1> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-new-oktaauthconfig" class="anchor" href="#new-oktaauthconfig" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>new OktaAuth(config)</h2> 
         <p>Creates a new instance of the Okta Auth Client with the provided options. The client has many <a href="#client-configuration">config options</a>. The only required option to get started is <code>url</code>, the base url for your Okta domain.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>config</code> - Options that are used to configure the client</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> authClient <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">OktaAuth</span>({url<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://acme.okta.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-signinoptions" class="anchor" href="#signinoptions" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>signIn(options)</h2> 
         <p>The goal of an authentication flow is to <a href="http://developer.okta.com/use_cases/authentication/session_cookie#retrieving-a-session-cookie-by-visiting-a-session-redirect-link">set an Okta session cookie on the user's browser</a> or <a href="http://developer.okta.com/use_cases/authentication/session_cookie#retrieving-a-session-cookie-via-openid-connect-authorization-endpoint">retrieve an <code>id_token</code> or <code>access_token</code></a>. The flow is started using <code>signIn</code>.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>username</code> - User’s non-qualified short-name (e.g. dade.murphy) or unique fully-qualified login (e.g <a href="mailto:dade.murphy@example.com">dade.murphy@example.com</a>)</li> 
          <li><code>password</code> - The password of the user</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-en">signIn</span>({
  username<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>some-username<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  password<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>some-password<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
})
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">===</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SUCCESS<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) {
    <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">session</span>.<span class="pl-en">setCookieAndRedirect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-smi">sessionToken</span>); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Sets a cookie on redirect</span>
  } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
    <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>We cannot handle the <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> status<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
  }
})
.<span class="pl-en">fail</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">error</span>(err);
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-signout" class="anchor" href="#signout" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>signOut()</h2> 
         <p>Signs the user out of their current Okta <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/sessions.html#example">session</a>.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-en">signOut</span>()
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>() {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>successfully logged out<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
})
.<span class="pl-en">fail</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">error</span>(err);
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-forgotpasswordoptions" class="anchor" href="#forgotpasswordoptions" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a><a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html#forgot-password">forgotPassword(options)</a></h2> 
         <p>Starts a new password recovery transaction for a given user and issues a recovery token that can be used to reset a user’s password.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>username</code> - User’s non-qualified short-name (e.g. dade.murphy) or unique fully-qualified login (e.g <a href="mailto:dade.murphy@example.com">dade.murphy@example.com</a>)</li> 
          <li><code>factorType</code> - Recovery factor to use for primary authentication. Supported options are <code>SMS</code>, <code>EMAIL</code>, or <code>CALL</code></li> 
          <li><code>relayState</code> - Optional state value that is persisted for the lifetime of the recovery transaction</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-en">forgotPassword</span>({
  username<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>dade.murphy@example.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  factorType<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SMS<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
})
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-en">verify</span>({
    passCode<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>123456<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> The passCode from the SMS or CALL</span>
  });
})
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">===</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SUCCESS<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) {
    <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">session</span>.<span class="pl-en">setCookieAndRedirect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-smi">sessionToken</span>);
  } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
    <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>We cannot handle the <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> status<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
  }
})
.<span class="pl-en">fail</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">error</span>(err);
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-unlockaccountoptions" class="anchor" href="#unlockaccountoptions" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a><a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html#unlock-account">unlockAccount(options)</a></h2> 
         <p>Starts a new unlock recovery transaction for a given user and issues a recovery token that can be used to unlock a user’s account.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>username</code> - User’s non-qualified short-name (e.g. dade.murphy) or unique fully-qualified login (e.g <a href="mailto:dade.murphy@example.com">dade.murphy@example.com</a>)</li> 
          <li><code>factorType</code> - Recovery factor to use for primary authentication. Supported options are <code>SMS</code>, <code>EMAIL</code>, or <code>CALL</code></li> 
          <li><code>relayState</code> - Optional state value that is persisted for the lifetime of the recovery transaction</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-en">unlockAccount</span>({
  username<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>dade.murphy@example.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  factorType<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SMS<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
})
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-en">verify</span>({
    passCode<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>123456<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> The passCode from the SMS</span>
  });
})
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">===</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SUCCESS<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) {
    <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">session</span>.<span class="pl-en">setCookieAndRedirect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-smi">sessionToken</span>);
  } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
    <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>We cannot handle the <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> status<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
  }
})
.<span class="pl-en">fail</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">error</span>(err);
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-verifyrecoverytokenoptions" class="anchor" href="#verifyrecoverytokenoptions" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a><a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html#verify-recovery-token">verifyRecoveryToken(options)</a></h2> 
         <p>Validates a recovery token that was distributed to the end-user to continue the recovery transaction.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>recoveryToken</code> - Recovery token that was distributed to end-user via an out-of-band mechanism such as email</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-en">verifyRecoveryToken</span>({
  recoveryToken<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>00xdqXOE5qDZX8-PBR1bYv8AESqIFinDy3yul01tyh<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
})
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">===</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SUCCESS<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) {
    <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">session</span>.<span class="pl-en">setCookieAndRedirect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-smi">sessionToken</span>);
  } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
    <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>We cannot handle the <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> status<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
  }
})
.<span class="pl-en">fail</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">error</span>(err);
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-txresume" class="anchor" href="#txresume" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>tx.resume()</h2> 
         <p>Resumes an in-progress <strong>transaction</strong>. This is useful if a user navigates away from the login page before authentication is complete.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> exists <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tx</span>.<span class="pl-en">exists</span>();
<span class="pl-k">if</span> (exists) {
  <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tx</span>.<span class="pl-en">resume</span>()
  .<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>) {
    <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>current status:<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-c1">status</span>);
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">fail</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
    <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">error</span>(err);
  });
}</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-txexists" class="anchor" href="#txexists" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>tx.exists()</h2> 
         <p>Check for a <strong>transaction</strong> to be resumed. This is synchronous and returns <code>true</code> or <code>false</code>.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> exists <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tx</span>.<span class="pl-en">exists</span>()
<span class="pl-k">if</span> (exists) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a session exists<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
} <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a session does not exist<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
}</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-transactionstatus" class="anchor" href="#transactionstatus" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>transaction.status</h2> 
         <p>When Auth Client methods resolve, they return a <strong>transaction</strong> object that encapsulates <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html#transaction-model">the new state in the authentication flow</a>. This <strong>transaction</strong> contains metadata about the current state, and methods that can be used to progress to the next state.</p> 
         <p><a href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b94a4d30a814b0fd07cebcade875875f9e2dc9a9/687474703a2f2f646576656c6f7065722e6f6b74612e636f6d2f6173736574732f696d672f617574682d73746174652d6d6f64656c2e706e67" target="_blank"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b94a4d30a814b0fd07cebcade875875f9e2dc9a9/687474703a2f2f646576656c6f7065722e6f6b74612e636f6d2f6173736574732f696d672f617574682d73746174652d6d6f64656c2e706e67" alt="State Model Diagram" title="State Model Diagram" data-canonical-src="http://developer.okta.com/assets/img/auth-state-model.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p> 
         <p>Sample transactions and their methods:</p> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-common-methods" class="anchor" href="#common-methods" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Common methods</h3> 
         <h4><a id="user-content-cancel" class="anchor" href="#cancel" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>cancel()</h4> 
         <p>Terminates the current auth flow.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-en">cancel</span>()
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>() {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> transaction canceled. You can now start another with authClient.signIn</span>
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-locked_out" class="anchor" href="#locked_out" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a><a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html#show-lockout-failures">LOCKED_OUT</a></h3> 
         <p>The user account is locked; self-service unlock or admin unlock is required.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre>{
  status<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>LOCKED_OUT<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-en">unlock</span><span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">options</span>) { <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> returns another transaction <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span> },
  <span class="pl-en">cancel</span><span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span>() { <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> terminates the auth flow <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span> },
  data<span class="pl-k">:</span> { <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> the parsed json response <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span> }
}</pre>
         </div> 
         <h4><a id="user-content-unlockoptions" class="anchor" href="#unlockoptions" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a><a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html#unlock-account">unlock(options)</a></h4> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>username</code> - User’s non-qualified short-name (e.g. dade.murphy) or unique fully-qualified login (e.g <a href="mailto:dade.murphy@example.com">dade.murphy@example.com</a>)</li> 
          <li><code>factorType</code> - Recovery factor to use for primary authentication. Supported options are <code>SMS</code>, <code>EMAIL</code>, or <code>CALL</code></li> 
          <li><code>relayState</code> - Optional state value that is persisted for the lifetime of the recovery transaction</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-en">unlock</span>({
  username<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>dade.murphy@example.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  factorType<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>EMAIL<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
});</pre>
         </div>

           </svg></a><a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/authn.html#change-password">changePassword(options)</a></h4> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>oldPassword</code> - User’s current password that is about to expire</li>

           </svg></a><a href="#cancel">cancel()</a></h4> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-success" class="anchor" href="#success" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>SUCCESS</h3> 
         <p>The end of the authentication flow! This transaction contains a sessionToken you can exchange for an Okta cookie, an <code>id_token</code>, or <code>access_token</code>.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre>{
  expiresAt<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>2015-06-08T23:34:34.000Z<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  status<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>SUCCESS<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  sessionToken<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>00p8RhRDCh_8NxIin-wtF5M6ofFtRhfKWGBAbd2WmE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  user<span class="pl-k">:</span> {
    id<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>00uhm5QzwyZZxjrfp0g3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
    profile<span class="pl-k">:</span> {
      login<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>exampleUser@example.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
      firstName<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Test<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
      lastName<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>User<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
      locale<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>en_US<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
      timeZone<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>America/Los_Angeles<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
    }
  }
}</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-sessionsetcookieandredirectsessiontoken-redirecturi" class="anchor" href="#sessionsetcookieandredirectsessiontoken-redirecturi" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>session.setCookieAndRedirect(sessionToken, redirectUri)</h2> 
         <p>This allows you to create a session using a sessionToken.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>sessionToken</code> - Ephemeral one-time token used to bootstrap an Okta session.</li> 
          <li><code>redirectUri</code> - After setting a cookie, Okta redirects to the specified URI. The default is the current URI.</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">session</span>.<span class="pl-en">setCookieAndRedirect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">transaction</span>.<span class="pl-smi">sessionToken</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-sessionexists" class="anchor" href="#sessionexists" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>session.exists()</h2> 
         <p>Returns a promise that resolves with <code>true</code> if there is an existing Okta <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/sessions.html#example">session</a>, or <code>false</code> if not.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">session</span>.<span class="pl-en">exists</span>()
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">exists</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> (exists) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> logged in</span>
  } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> not logged in</span>
  }
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-sessionget" class="anchor" href="#sessionget" aria-hidden="true">

         <h2><a id="user-content-sessionrefresh" class="anchor" href="#sessionrefresh" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>session.refresh()</h2> 
         <p>Refresh the current session by extending its lifetime. This can be used as a keep-alive operation.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">session</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>()
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">session</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> existing session is now refreshed</span>
})
.<span class="pl-en">catch</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> there was a problem refreshing (the user may not have an existing session)</span>
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokengetwithoutpromptoauthoptions" class="anchor" href="#tokengetwithoutpromptoauthoptions" aria-hidden="true">

           </svg></a>token.getWithoutPrompt(oauthOptions)</h2> 
         <p>When you've obtained a sessionToken from the authorization flows, or a session already exists, you can obtain a token or tokens without prompting the user to log in.</p>

         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">

  responseType<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>id_token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> or array of types</span>
  sessionToken<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>testSessionToken<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> optional if the user has an existing Okta session</span>
})
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tokenOrTokens</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> manage token or tokens</span>
})
.<span class="pl-en">catch</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> handle OAuthError</span>
});</pre>
         </div>

         <h2><a id="user-content-tokendecodeidtokenstring" class="anchor" href="#tokendecodeidtokenstring" aria-hidden="true">

         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenrefreshtokentorefresh" class="anchor" href="#tokenrefreshtokentorefresh" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>token.refresh(tokenToRefresh)</h2> 
         <p>Returns a new token if the Okta <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/sessions.html#example">session</a> is still valid.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>tokenToRefresh</code> - an access token or ID token previously provided by Okta. note: this is not the raw JWT</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> this token is provided by Okta via getWithoutPrompt, getWithPopup, and parseFromUrl</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> tokenToRefresh <span class="pl-k">=</span> {
  idToken<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR_ID_TOKEN_JWT<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  claims<span class="pl-k">:</span> { <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> token claims <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span> },
  expiresAt<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">1449699930</span>,
  scopes<span class="pl-k">:</span> [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>openid<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>email<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
  authorizeUrl<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://example.okta.com/oauth2/v1/authorize<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  issuer<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://example.okta.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  clientId<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>NPSfOkH5eZrTy8PMDlvx<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
};

<span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">token</span>.<span class="pl-en">refresh</span>(tokenToRefresh)
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">freshToken</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> manage freshToken</span>
})
.<span class="pl-en">catch</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> handle OAuthError</span>
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokengetuserinfoaccesstokenobject" class="anchor" href="#tokengetuserinfoaccesstokenobject" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>token.getUserInfo(accessTokenObject)</h2> 
         <p>Retrieve the <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/oidc.html#response-example-success">details about a user</a>.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>accessTokenObject</code> - an access token returned by this library. note: this is not the raw access token</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">token</span>.<span class="pl-en">getUserInfo</span>(accessTokenObject)
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">user</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> user has details about the user</span>
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenverifyidtokenobject" class="anchor" href="#tokenverifyidtokenobject" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>token.verify(idTokenObject)</h2> 
         <p>Verify the validity of an ID token's claims and check the signature on browsers that support web cryptography.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>idTokenObject</code> - an ID token returned by this library. note: this is not the raw ID token JWT</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">token</span>.<span class="pl-en">verify</span>(idTokenObject)
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>() {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> the idToken is valid</span>
})
.<span class="pl-en">catch</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> handle AuthSdkError</span>
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenmanageraddkey-token" class="anchor" href="#tokenmanageraddkey-token" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>tokenManager.add(key, token)</h2> 
         <p>After receiving an <code>access_token</code> or <code>id_token</code>, add it to the <code>tokenManager</code> to manage token expiration and refresh operations. When a token is added to the <code>tokenManager</code>, it is automatically refreshed when it expires.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>key</code> - Unique key to store the token in the <code>tokenManager</code>. This is used later when you want to get, delete, or refresh the token.</li> 
          <li><code>token</code> - Token object that will be added</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">token</span>.<span class="pl-en">getWithPopup</span>()
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">idToken</span>) {
  <span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-c1">add</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>my_id_token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, idToken);
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenmanagergetkey" class="anchor" href="#tokenmanagergetkey" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>tokenManager.get(key)</h2> 
         <p>Get a token that you have previously added to the <code>tokenManager</code> with the given <code>key</code>.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>key</code> - Key for the token you want to get</li>

         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">

         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenmanagerremovekey" class="anchor" href="#tokenmanagerremovekey" aria-hidden="true">

          <li><code>key</code> - Key for the token you want to remove</li>

         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">

         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenmanagerclear" class="anchor" href="#tokenmanagerclear" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>

         <p>Remove all tokens from the <code>tokenManager</code>.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-c1">clear</span>();</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenmanagerrefreshkey" class="anchor" href="#tokenmanagerrefreshkey" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>tokenManager.refresh(key)</h2> 
         <p>Manually refresh a token before it expires.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>key</code> - Key for the token you want to refresh</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Because the refresh() method is async, you can wait for it to complete</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> by using the returned Promise:</span>
<span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">refresh</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>my_id_token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
.<span class="pl-en">then</span>(<span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">newToken</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> doSomethingWith(newToken);</span>
});

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Alternatively, you can subscribe to the 'refreshed' event:</span>
<span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">on</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>refreshed<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">key</span>, <span class="pl-smi">newToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">oldToken</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> doSomethingWith(newToken);</span>
});
<span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">refresh</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>my_id_token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenmanageronevent-callback-context" class="anchor" href="#tokenmanageronevent-callback-context" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>tokenManager.on(event, callback[, context])</h2> 
         <p>Subscribe to an event published by the <code>tokenManager</code>.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>event</code> - Event to subscribe to. Possible events are <code>expired</code>, <code>error</code>, and <code>refreshed</code>.</li> 
          <li><code>callback</code> - Function to call when the event is triggered</li> 
          <li><code>context</code> - Optional context to bind the callback to</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">on</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>expired<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">key</span>, <span class="pl-smi">expiredToken</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Token with key<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, key, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> has expired:<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(expiredToken);
});

<span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">on</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>error<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>TokenManager error:<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, err);
});

<span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">on</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>refreshed<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">key</span>, <span class="pl-smi">newToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">oldToken</span>) {
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Token with key<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, key, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>has been refreshed<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Old token:<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, oldToken);
  <span class="pl-en">console</span>.<span class="pl-c1">log</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>New token:<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, newToken);
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-tokenmanageroffevent-callback" class="anchor" href="#tokenmanageroffevent-callback" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>tokenManager.off(event[, callback])</h2> 
         <p>Unsubscribe from <code>tokenManager</code> events. If no callback is provided, unsubscribes all listeners from the event.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>event</code> - Event to unsubscribe from</li> 
          <li><code>callback</code> - Optional callback that was used to subscribe to the event</li> 
         </ul> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">off</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>refreshed<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);
<span class="pl-smi">authClient</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tokenManager</span>.<span class="pl-en">off</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>refreshed<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, myRefreshedCallback);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h1><a id="user-content-client-configuration" class="anchor" href="#client-configuration" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Client Configuration</h1> 
         <p>The only required configuration option is <code>url</code>. All others are optional.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> config <span class="pl-k">=</span> {
  url<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://your-org.okta.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  clientId<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>your-client-id<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  redirectUri<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://your.redirect.uri/redirect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
};

<span class="pl-k">var</span> authClient <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">OktaAuth</span>(config);</pre>
         </div> 
         <ul> 
          <li> <p><strong>url:</strong> The URL for your Okta organization</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Production org with subdomain "acme"</span>
url<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://acme.okta.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Can also target oktapreview and okta-emea, i.e.</span>
url<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://acme.oktapreview.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>ajaxRequest</strong> The ajax request implementation. By default, this is implemented using <a href="https://github.com/ded/reqwest">reqwest</a>. To provide your own request library, implement the following interface:</p> 
           <ol> 
            <li>Must accept:</li> 
           </ol> 
           <ul> 
            <li>method (http method)</li> 
            <li>url (target url)</li> 
            <li>args (object containing headers and data)</li> 
           </ul> 
           <ol start="2"> 
            <li>Must return a Promise that resolves with a raw XMLHttpRequest response</li> 
           </ol> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre><span class="pl-en">ajaxRequest</span><span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">method</span>, <span class="pl-smi">url</span>, <span class="pl-smi">args</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span></span>
<span class="pl-c">  args is in the form:</span>
<span class="pl-c">  {</span>
<span class="pl-c">    headers: {</span>
<span class="pl-c">      headerName: headerValue</span>
<span class="pl-c">    },</span>
<span class="pl-c">    data: postBodyData</span>
<span class="pl-c">  }</span>
<span class="pl-c">  <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">Promise</span>.<span class="pl-en">resolve</span>(<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> a raw XMLHttpRequest response <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>);
}</pre>
           </div> <p>If you're using a bundler like webpack or browserify, we have implementations for jquery and reqwest included. To use them, import the SDK like this:</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> reqwest</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> OktaAuth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>@okta/okta-auth-js/reqwest<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> jquery</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> OktaAuth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>@okta/okta-auth-js/jquery<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
           </div> </li> 
         </ul> 
         <h1><a id="user-content-openid-connect-options" class="anchor" href="#openid-connect-options" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>OpenId Connect Options</h1> 
         <p>Options for the <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/oidc.html">OpenId Connect</a> authentication flow. This flow is required for social authentication, and requires OAuth client registration with Okta. For instructions, see <a href="http://developer.okta.com/docs/api/resources/social_authentication.html">Social Authentication</a>.</p> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-can-be-in-client-configuration" class="anchor" href="#can-be-in-client-configuration" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Can be in Client Configuration</h2> 
         <p>These configuration options can be included when instantiating Okta Auth JS (<code>new OktaAuth(config)</code>) or in <code>token.getWithoutPrompt</code>, <code>token.getWithPopup</code>, or <code>token.getWithRedirect</code>. If included in both, the value passed in the method takes priority.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li> <p><strong>clientId:</strong> Client Id pre-registered with Okta for the OIDC authentication flow.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>clientId<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>GHtf9iJdr60A9IYrR0jw<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>redirectUri:</strong> The url that is redirected to when using <code>token.getWithRedirect</code>. This must be pre-registered as part of client registration. If no <code>redirectUri</code> is provided, defaults to the current origin.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>redirectUri<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://acme.com/oauth2/callback/home<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>issuer:</strong> Specify a custom issuer to perform the OIDC flow. Defaults to the baseUrl.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>issuer<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://your-org.okta.com/oauth2/aus8aus76q8iphupD0h7<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>authorizeUrl:</strong> Specify a custom authorizeUrl to perform the OIDC flow. Defaults to the issuer plus "/v1/authorize".</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>issuer<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://your-org.okta.com/oauth2/aus8aus76q8iphupD0h7<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
authorizeUrl<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://your-org.okta.com/oauth2/aus8aus76q8iphupD0h7/v1/authorize<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>userinfoUrl:</strong> Specify a custom authorizeUrl to perform the OIDC flow. Defaults to the issuer plus "/v1/userinfo".</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>issuer<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://your-org.okta.com/oauth2/aus8aus76q8iphupD0h7<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
userinfoUrl<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://your-org.okta.com/oauth2/aus8aus76q8iphupD0h7/v1/userinfo<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
         </ul> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-cannot-be-in-client-configuration" class="anchor" href="#cannot-be-in-client-configuration" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Cannot be in Client Configuration</h2> 
         <ul> 
          <li> <p><strong>sessionToken</strong> Specify an Okta sessionToken to skip reauthentication when the user already authenticated using the Authentication Flow.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>sessionToken<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>00p8RhRDCh_8NxIin-wtF5M6ofFtRhfKWGBAbd2WmE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>responseMode:</strong> Specify how the authorization response should be returned. You will generally not need to set this unless you want to override the default values for <code>token.getWithRedirect</code>.</p> 
           <ul> 
            <li> <p><code>okta_post_message</code> - Used with <code>token.getWithPopup</code> and <code>token.getWithoutPrompt</code>. Uses <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Window/postMessage">postMessage</a> to send the response from the popup or iframe to the origin window.</p> </li> 
            <li> <p><code>fragment</code> - Default value when using <code>token.getWithRedirect</code> and <code>responseType != 'code'</code>. Returns the authorization response in the hash fragment of the URL after the authorization redirect.</p> </li> 
            <li> <p><code>query</code> - Default value when using <code>token.getWithRedirect</code> and <code>responseType = 'code'</code>. Returns the authorization response in the query string of the URL after the authorization redirect.</p> </li> 
            <li> <p><code>form_post</code> - Returns the authorization response as a form POST after the authorization redirect. Use this when using <code>token.getWithRedirect</code> and you do not want the response returned in the URL.</p> </li> 
           </ul> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Use form_post instead of query in the Authorization Code flow</span>
responseType<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>code<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
responseMode<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>form_post<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>responseType:</strong> Specify the response type for OIDC authentication. Defaults to <code>id_token</code>.</p> <p>Valid response types are <code>id_token</code>, <code>access_token</code>, and <code>code</code>. Note that <code>code</code> goes through the Authorization Code flow, which requires the server to exchange the Authorization Code for tokens.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Specifying a single responseType</span>
responseType<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Use an array if specifying multiple response types - in this case,</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> the response will contain both an ID Token and an Access Token.</span>
responseType<span class="pl-k">:</span> [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>id_token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>]</pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>scopes:</strong> Specify what information to make available in the returned <code>id_token</code> or <code>access_token</code>. For OIDC, you must include <code>openid</code> as one of the scopes. Defaults to <code>['openid', 'email']</code>.</p> <p>Valid OIDC scopes: <code>openid</code>, <code>email</code>, <code>profile</code>, <code>address</code>, <code>phone</code>, <code>groups</code>, <code>offline_access</code></p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>scopes<span class="pl-k">:</span> [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>openid<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>email<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>profile<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>address<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>phone<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>groups<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>offline_access<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>]</pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>state:</strong> Specify a state that will be validated in an OAuth response. This is usually only provided during redirect flows to obtain an authorization code. Defaults to a random string.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>state<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>8rFzn3MH5q<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p><strong>nonce:</strong> Specify a nonce that will be validated in an <code>id_token</code>. This is usually only provided during redirect flows to obtain an authorization code that will be exchanged for an <code>id_token</code>. Defaults to a random string.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre>nonce<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>51GePTswrm<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
         </ul> 
         <h1><a id="user-content-developing-the-okta-auth-client" class="anchor" href="#developing-the-okta-auth-client" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Developing the Okta Auth Client</h1> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-building-the-client" class="anchor" href="#building-the-client" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Building the Client</h2> 
         <ol> 
          <li> <p>Clone the repo.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell">
            <pre>[path]$ git clone git@github.com:okta/okta-auth-js.git</pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p>Navigate to the new <code>okta-auth-js</code> folder, and install the Okta node dependencies.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell">
            <pre>[path/okta-auth-js]$ npm install</pre>
           </div> </li> 
          <li> <p>Build the SDK. The output will be under <code>dist/browser/</code>. The standalone version is <code>okta-auth-js.min.js</code>.</p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell">
            <pre>[path/okta-auth-js]$ npm run build</pre>
           </div> </li> 
         </ol> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-build-and-test-commands" class="anchor" href="#build-and-test-commands" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Build and Test Commands</h2> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Command</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>npm run build</code></td> 
            <td>Build the SDK with a sourcemap</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>npm test</code></td> 
            <td>Run unit tests using PhantomJS</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>npm run lint:report</code></td> 
            <td>Run eslint linting tests</td> 
           </tr>
          </tbody>
         </table>
